<p>Include this prompt in your AI assistant to guide consistent code generation for Turborepo + Prisma + Prisma Postgres projects.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>GitHub Copilot</strong>: Type <code>#&lt;filename&gt;</code> to reference the prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Cursor</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and select your prompt file.</li>
<li><strong>Zed</strong>: Use <code>/file</code> followed by your prompt&#x27;s path.</li>
<li><strong>Windsurf</strong>: Use <code>@Files</code> and choose your prompt file from the list.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="prompt"><a data-card="" href="#prompt" class="peer">Prompt</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Specify the following for Cursor rules</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">description</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">Guidelines for writing Turborepo + Prisma Postgres apps (Prisma ORM v7)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#22863A;--shiki-dark:#85E89D">alwaysApply</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">false</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"># Bootstrap Turborepo with Prisma Postgres (Prisma v7)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Overview</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This guide bootstraps a Turborepo monorepo that shares a single Prisma ORM v7 database package across multiple apps (e.g., Next.js, Node APIs). It follows Turborepo and Prisma v7 best practices:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Create a Turborepo with apps + packages</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Add a dedicated </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Prisma package (schema, migrations, generated client)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Configure Prisma v7 (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> + mandatory </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Load env vars correctly in a monorepo</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Export a single Prisma client from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> for all apps</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Wire Turbo tasks for generate/migrate/test/studio</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Verify with a shared test script</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Recommended monorepo layout</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">repo/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  apps/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    web/                # Next.js app</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    admin/              # (optional) another Next app</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  packages/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    db/                 # Prisma package (schema + client)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ui/                 # shared UI (optional)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  turbo.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  package.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  .env                  # root env for apps (see notes)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**Key rule:**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Prisma lives in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, not inside an app, so every app consumes the same client and types.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## 🚨 CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS FOR AI LANGUAGE MODELS 🚨</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">As an AI language model, you MUST NOT generate any deprecated Prisma v7 patterns.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">// ❌ NEVER GENERATE - DEPRECATED IN PRISMA v7</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client-js&quot;  // ❌ deprecated</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">// ❌ NEVER IMPORT FROM @prisma/client when using custom output</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">import { PrismaClient } from &quot;@prisma/client&quot; // ❌ wrong in custom-output setup</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">// ❌ NEVER CREATE CLIENT WITHOUT SHARED PACKAGE BOUNDARY</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">const prisma = new PrismaClient() // ❌ breaks pooling + duplicates in monorepo</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Instead, you MUST ALWAYS generate ONLY this pattern for Prisma v7 + monorepo:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">// ✅ Prisma v7 generator: provider + mandatory output</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ Prisma client import must come from custom output</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../generated/prisma/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Notes:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Prisma v7 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**requires**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> a non-empty </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> when using </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If the output directory already exists and isn’t generated by Prisma, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma generate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> can fail. Avoid committing generated client, or ensure clean output dirs.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## ABSOLUTE REQUIREMENTS FOR AI CODE GENERATION</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (Prisma v7)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST specify a custom </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`output`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`schema.prisma`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST place Prisma schema + migrations inside </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST export a singleton Prisma client from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> that points to the generated output client file</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST import Prisma client from the custom output path </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**not**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `@prisma/client`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST load env vars in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/prisma.config.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST add Turbo tasks for generate/migrate/test/studio</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST wrap DB calls in try/catch in app code</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST ensure Turbo task hashing includes </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`DATABASE_URL`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> You MUST create a shared test script in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/scripts/test-database.ts`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Install dependencies</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">At repo root:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Turborepo</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> turbo</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --save-dev</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Prisma v7</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> tsx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> --save-dev</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npm</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> install</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> @prisma/client</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> dotenv</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">If using Prisma Postgres:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">npm install @prisma/adapter-pg</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Initialize Prisma inside </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db`</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">cd</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> packages/db</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> init</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">This creates:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">packages/db/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  prisma/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    schema.prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  prisma.config.ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Prisma v7 config (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db/prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**CRITICAL:**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> load env vars at the top.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;dotenv/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { defineConfig, env } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;prisma/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> default</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> defineConfig</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  schema: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma/schema.prisma&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  migrations: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    path: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;prisma/migrations&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  datasource: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    url: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">env</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;DATABASE_URL&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Prisma schema (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  output   = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">datasource db {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  provider = &quot;postgresql&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">model User {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  id        Int      @id @default(autoincrement())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  email     String   @unique</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  name      String?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  createdAt DateTime @default(now())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Shared Prisma client singleton (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db/src/client.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">)</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../generated/prisma/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//Prisma Driver Adapter for Postgres</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaPg } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@prisma/adapter-pg&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Create a new Driver Adapter instance for PrismaPostgres</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> adapter</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaPg</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  connectionString: process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">DATABASE_URL</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">!</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> globalForPrisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalThis </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">  prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">?:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">};</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> prisma</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> globalForPrisma.prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">??</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> PrismaClient</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ adapter });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (process.env.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">NODE_ENV</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> !==</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;production&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Root scripts (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`package.json`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">)</span></span>
