<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;scripts&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;dev&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo dev&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo build&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;lint&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo lint&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:generate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo run db:generate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:push&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo run db:push&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:migrate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo run db:migrate&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:studio&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo run db:studio&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;db:test&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;turbo run db:test&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Shared test script (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db/scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;dotenv/config&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;../src/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> testDatabase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;🔍 Testing Prisma Postgres connection...</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;✅ Connected to database!&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">📝 Creating a test user...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> newUser</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">create</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      data: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        email: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;demo@example.com&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">        name: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Demo User&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;✅ Created user:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, newUser);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">📋 Fetching all users...&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> allUsers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">findMany</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`✅ Found ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">allUsers</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} user(s):`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    allUsers.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">forEach</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">((</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">      console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">`   - ${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">name</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">} (${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">user</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">email</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">})`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">🎉 All tests passed! Your database is working.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">\n</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (error) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;❌ Error:&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, error);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    process.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">exit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">finally</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$disconnect</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">testDatabase</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Using Prisma in apps (example: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`apps/web`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> Next.js)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">In any app, add a dependency on </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@repo/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (workspace):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;dependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;@repo/db&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;*&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Then in server-side code:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { prisma } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@repo/db&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { NextResponse } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;next/server&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> GET</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  try</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> users</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> prisma.user.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">findMany</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NextResponse.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">json</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(users);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">catch</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (e) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    console.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">error</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(e);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> NextResponse.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">json</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ error: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;Failed to fetch users&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> }, { status: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">500</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## Complete setup workflow</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Create Turborepo**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (or use existing):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```npm</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npx create-turbo@latest</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, install Prisma v7 deps.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Initialize Prisma in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   cd packages/db</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npx prisma init</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Update </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to include </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Update schema**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with Prisma v7 generator + output.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Create </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`src/client.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> singleton and export via </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`src/index.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Wire Turbo tasks**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`turbo.json`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Add </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> at root </span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**and/or**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `packages/db/.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Push schema**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   npm run db:push</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">   ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Test**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    npm run db:test</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">11.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Start dev**</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    npm run dev</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    ```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI Model verification checklist</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Before generating any code, verify:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `output   = &quot;../src/generated/prisma&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> present?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> All Prisma files in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Client imports from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`../generated/prisma/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> (or via </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@repo/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Turbo tasks depend on </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:generate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> listed in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`globalEnv`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> All DB ops wrapped in try/catch?</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Test script exists in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">?</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">No exceptions. If any check fails, STOP and FIX.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">## AI MODEL RESPONSE TEMPLATE (UPDATED FOR TURBOREPO + PRISMA v7)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">When asked about implementing Prisma v7 inside a Turborepo monorepo (with any framework such as Next.js, Node, etc.), you MUST:</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">1.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Assume Prisma lives in a shared package**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Always place schema, config, and migrations in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Never suggest adding Prisma directly into an app unless the user explicitly says they don’t want a shared package.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">2.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Use only Prisma v7 generator patterns**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> The schema MUST include:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```prisma</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     generator client {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">       provider = &quot;prisma-client&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">       output   = &quot;./generated/prisma&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Never use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`prisma-client-js`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">3.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Use correct import paths for custom output**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Any PrismaClient import MUST come from the generated output:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">     import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { PrismaClient } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;./generated/prisma/client&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If importing from apps, you MUST import via the package boundary:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```ts</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">     import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { prisma } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;@repo/db&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">     ```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Never import from </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`@prisma/client`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in this setup.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Always include a shared singleton client in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold">**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Provide a </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/src/client.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> with global caching for dev hot-reload.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If Accelerate is requested or implied, use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`$extends(withAccelerate())`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If Accelerate is not requested, omit it.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">5.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Always load environment variables properly**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `packages/db/prisma.config.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> MUST start with </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`import &quot;dotenv/config&quot;`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Use </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`process.env.DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> in runtime code.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Remind users that </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`.env`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> should exist at root and/or </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">6.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Always wire Turbo dependencies**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Turbo tasks </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`dev`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`build`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> MUST depend on </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`^db:generate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> `DATABASE_URL`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> MUST be listed in </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`globalEnv`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> to ensure correct task hashing.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">7.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Provide correct repo-level scripts**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Root scripts should proxy to Turbo (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`turbo run db:*`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">).</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> The Prisma package </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> should own </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:generate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:migrate`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:studio`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, and </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`db:test`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">8.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Include a real verification step**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Provide (or reference) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`packages/db/scripts/test-database.ts`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Ensure it imports dotenv and disconnects Prisma on completion.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">9.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Use safe runtime patterns**</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> All DB calls in apps MUST be wrapped in try/catch.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">   -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> In Next.js App Router examples, use server-only imports and return </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">`NextResponse`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">10.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-light-font-weight:bold;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;--shiki-dark-font-weight:bold"> **Self-verify before replying**</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> Re-check all items in the “AI Model verification checklist.”</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">-</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> If any item is missing or incorrect, STOP and FIX before responding.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">Remember: There are NO exceptions to these rules. Every requirement is mandatory for a correct Turborepo + Prisma v7 setup.</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2" id="running-the-application"><a data-card="" href="#running-the-application" class="peer">Running the application</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Get your application running locally in three quick steps:</p>
<p><strong>1. Generate the Prisma Client:</strong></p>
<figure dir="ltr" class="my-4 bg-fd-card rounded-square shiki relative border border-stroke-neutral not-prose overflow-hidden text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="-1"><div class="empty:hidden absolute top-3 right-2 z-2 backdrop-blur-lg rounded-lg text-fd-muted-foreground"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-fd-ring p-1 [&amp;_svg]:size-4 hover:text-fd-accent-foreground data-checked:text-fd-accent-foreground" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-clipboard" aria-hidden="true"><rect width="8" height="4" x="8" y="2" rx="1" ry="1"></rect><path d="M16 4h2a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H6a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h2"></path></svg></button></div><div role="region" tabindex="0" class="text-[0.8125rem] py-3.5 overflow-auto max-h-[600px] fd-scroll-container focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-inset focus-visible:ring-fd-ring bg-background-default" style="--padding-right:calc(var(--spacing) * 8)"><pre class="min-w-full w-max *:flex *:flex-col"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">npx</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> turbo</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> db:generate</span></span></code></pre></div></figure>
<p><strong>2. View your database in Prisma Studio:</strong></p>
<div dir="ltr" data-orientation="horizontal" class="bg-background-default rounded-square border border-stroke-neutral overflow-hidden my-4"><div role="tablist" aria-orientation="horizontal"
